
```sql
-- 创建商品表  
CREATE TABLE Products (  
    ProductID INT PRIMARY KEY,  
    ProductName VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,  
    Specification VARCHAR2(255),  
    PurchaserID INT  
);  

DESC Products;
DESC Purchasers;
DESC PurchaseRecords;


-- 创建采购员表  
CREATE TABLE Purchasers (  
    PurchaserID INT PRIMARY KEY,  
    PurchaserName VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL  
);  

-- 创建采购记录表  
CREATE TABLE PurchaseRecords (  
    ProductID INT NOT NULL,  
    PurchaseDate DATE NOT NULL,  
    PurchasePrice DECIMAL(10, 2) NOT NULL CHECK (PurchasePrice > 0),  
    PurchaseQuantity INT NOT NULL CHECK (PurchaseQuantity > 0),  
    PRIMARY KEY (ProductID, PurchaseDate),  
    FOREIGN KEY (ProductID) REFERENCES Products(ProductID)  
);
  
-- 为Products表添加外键约束到PurchaserID  
ALTER TABLE Products  
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_Products_PurchaserID FOREIGN KEY (PurchaserID) REFERENCES Purchasers(PurchaserID);
```

```sql
-- 插入采购员数据  
INSERT INTO Purchasers (PurchaserID, PurchaserName) VALUES (1, '张三');  
INSERT INTO Purchasers (PurchaserID, PurchaserName) VALUES (2, '李四');  
INSERT INTO Purchasers (PurchaserID, PurchaserName) VALUES (3, '王五');  
INSERT INTO Purchasers (PurchaserID, PurchaserName) VALUES (4, '赵六');  
  
-- 插入商品数据  
INSERT INTO Products (ProductID, ProductName, Specification, PurchaserID) VALUES (1001, '商品A', '规格A', 1);  
INSERT INTO Products (ProductID, ProductName, Specification, PurchaserID) VALUES (1002, '商品B', '规格B', 2);  
INSERT INTO Products (ProductID, ProductName, Specification, PurchaserID) VALUES (1003, '商品C', '规格C', 3);  
INSERT INTO Products (ProductID, ProductName, Specification, PurchaserID) VALUES (1004, '商品D', '规格D', 4);  
  
-- 插入采购记录数据  
INSERT INTO PurchaseRecords (ProductID, PurchaseDate, PurchasePrice, PurchaseQuantity) VALUES (1001, TO_DATE('2023-01-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 10.50, 5);  
INSERT INTO PurchaseRecords (ProductID, PurchaseDate, PurchasePrice, PurchaseQuantity) VALUES (1002, TO_DATE('2023-01-02', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 20.75, 3);  
INSERT INTO PurchaseRecords (ProductID, PurchaseDate, PurchasePrice, PurchaseQuantity) VALUES (1003, TO_DATE('2023-01-03', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 15.25, 2);  
INSERT INTO PurchaseRecords (ProductID, PurchaseDate, PurchasePrice, PurchaseQuantity) VALUES (1004, TO_DATE('2023-01-04', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 8.99, 10);  
  
-- 更新一条商品数据  
UPDATE Products SET Specification = '新规格A' WHERE ProductID = 1001;  
  
-- 删除一条采购记录数据  
DELETE FROM PurchaseRecords WHERE ProductID = 1001 AND PurchaseDate = TO_DATE('2023-01-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD');
```

```sql
-- 查询所有商品信息  
SELECT * FROM Products;  
  
-- 查询所有采购员信息  
SELECT * FROM Purchasers;  
  
-- 查询2023年1月购买的商品记录  
SELECT * FROM PurchaseRecords  
WHERE PurchaseDate BETWEEN TO_DATE('2023-01-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD') AND TO_DATE('2023-01-31', 'YYYY-MM-DD');
```




---
```sql
-- 创建 Employee 表  
CREATE TABLE Employee (  
    EmployeeID INT PRIMARY KEY,  
    Name VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,  
    DepartmentID INT  
);  
  
-- 创建 Department 表  
CREATE TABLE Department (  
    DepartmentID INT PRIMARY KEY,  
    DepartmentName VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL  
);  
  
-- 创建 MedicalCheckup 表  
CREATE TABLE MedicalCheckup (  
    EmployeeID INT,  
    CheckupDate DATE,  
    Hospital VARCHAR2(100),  
    GeneralResult VARCHAR2(255),  
    PRIMARY KEY (EmployeeID, CheckupDate),  
    FOREIGN KEY (EmployeeID) REFERENCES Employee(EmployeeID)  
);  
  
-- 创建 CheckupDetail 表  
CREATE TABLE CheckupDetail (  
    EmployeeID INT,  
    CheckupDate DATE,  
    CheckupItem VARCHAR2(100),  
    SubResult VARCHAR2(255),  
    PRIMARY KEY (EmployeeID, CheckupDate, CheckupItem),  
    FOREIGN KEY (EmployeeID, CheckupDate) REFERENCES MedicalCheckup(EmployeeID, CheckupDate)  
);  
  
-- 添加外键约束到 Employee 表  
ALTER TABLE Employee  

FOREIGN KEY (DepartmentID) REFERENCES Department(DepartmentID);
```

```sql
-- 插入 Department 数据  
INSERT INTO Department (DepartmentID, DepartmentName) VALUES (1, 'HR');  
INSERT INTO Department (DepartmentID, DepartmentName) VALUES (2, 'Engineering');  
INSERT INTO Department (DepartmentID, DepartmentName) VALUES (3, 'Finance');  
INSERT INTO Department (DepartmentID, DepartmentName) VALUES (4, 'Marketing');  
  
-- 插入 Employee 数据  
INSERT INTO Employee (EmployeeID, Name, DepartmentID) VALUES (1, 'John Doe', 1);  
INSERT INTO Employee (EmployeeID, Name, DepartmentID) VALUES (2, 'Jane Smith', 2);  
INSERT INTO Employee (EmployeeID, Name, DepartmentID) VALUES (3, 'Bob Johnson', 3);  
INSERT INTO Employee (EmployeeID, Name, DepartmentID) VALUES (4, 'Alice Brown', 4);  
  
-- 插入 MedicalCheckup 数据  
INSERT INTO MedicalCheckup (EmployeeID, CheckupDate, Hospital) VALUES (1, TO_DATE('2023-01-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 'Hospital A');  
INSERT INTO MedicalCheckup (EmployeeID, CheckupDate, Hospital) VALUES (2, TO_DATE('2023-02-15', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 'Hospital B');  
INSERT INTO MedicalCheckup (EmployeeID, CheckupDate, Hospital) VALUES (3, TO_DATE('2023-03-08', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 'Hospital A');  
INSERT INTO MedicalCheckup (EmployeeID, CheckupDate, Hospital) VALUES (4, TO_DATE('2023-04-22', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 'Hospital C');  
  
-- 插入 CheckupDetail 数据  
INSERT INTO CheckupDetail (EmployeeID, CheckupDate, CheckupItem, SubResult) VALUES (1, TO_DATE('2023-01-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 'Blood Test', 'Normal');  
INSERT INTO CheckupDetail (EmployeeID, CheckupDate, CheckupItem, SubResult) VALUES (1, TO_DATE('2023-01-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 'ECG', 'Abnormal');  
INSERT INTO CheckupDetail (EmployeeID, CheckupDate, CheckupItem, SubResult) VALUES (2, TO_DATE('2023-02-15', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 'X-Ray', 'Normal');  
INSERT INTO CheckupDetail (EmployeeID, CheckupDate, CheckupItem, SubResult) VALUES (3, TO_DATE('2023-03-08', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 'Blood Pressure', 'High'); 


-- 假设 GeneralResult 是基于 SubResult 的汇总结果，这里我们简单地随机设置一些值  
UPDATE MedicalCheckup   
SET GeneralResult = 'Good'   
WHERE EmployeeID = 1 AND CheckupDate = TO_DATE('2023-01-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD');  
  
UPDATE MedicalCheckup   
SET GeneralResult = 'Needs Attention'   
WHERE EmployeeID = 2 AND CheckupDate = TO_DATE('2023-02-15', 'YYYY-MM-DD');  
  
-- 类似地，您可以为其他员工和日期设置 GeneralResult


-- 更新 Employee 表中的 Name 列  
UPDATE Employee   
SET Name = 'John Doe Jr.'   
WHERE EmployeeID = 1;  
  
-- 更新 MedicalCheckup 表中的 Hospital 列  
UPDATE MedicalCheckup   
SET Hospital = 'New Hospital'   
WHERE EmployeeID = 2 AND CheckupDate = TO_DATE('2023-02-15', 'YYYY-MM-DD');


-- 删除 Employee 表中 EmployeeID 为 5 的行（假设存在）  
DELETE FROM Employee WHERE EmployeeID = 5;  
  
```

```sql
-- 查询所有员工的姓名和部门名称  
SELECT e.Name, d.DepartmentName   
FROM Employee e   
JOIN Department d ON e.DepartmentID = d.DepartmentID;  
  
-- 查询特定日期进行的所有体检的详细信息  
SELECT *   
FROM MedicalCheckup   
WHERE CheckupDate = TO_DATE('2023-01-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD');

DESC Employee

-- 查询所有员工的姓名、部门名称以及最近的体检日期  
SELECT e.Name, d.DepartmentName
FROM Employee e   
JOIN Department d ON e.DepartmentID = d.DepartmentID   
LEFT JOIN (  
    SELECT EmployeeID, MAX(CheckupDate) AS LatestCheckup   
    FROM MedicalCheckup   
    GROUP BY EmployeeID  
) mc ON e.EmployeeID = mc.EmployeeID;  
  
-- 查询特定员工在某个日期进行的体检的分项结果  
SELECT cd.CheckupItem, cd.SubResult   
FROM CheckupDetail cd   
JOIN MedicalCheckup mc ON cd.EmployeeID = mc.EmployeeID AND cd.CheckupDate = mc.CheckupDate   
WHERE mc.EmployeeID = 1 AND mc.CheckupDate = TO_DATE('2023-01-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD');
```






```sql
-- 创建学生表  
CREATE TABLE Students (  
    StudentID VARCHAR2(20) PRIMARY KEY,  
    Name VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,  
    Gender CHAR(1) CHECK (Gender IN ('M', 'F', 'O')),  
    Major VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,  
    Class VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,  
    DormitoryNumber VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,  
    AdministratorEmployeeID VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,  
    FOREIGN KEY (AdministratorEmployeeID) REFERENCES Administrators(EmployeeID)  
);  
  
-- 创建寝室表  
CREATE TABLE Dormitories (  
    DormitoryNumber VARCHAR2(20) PRIMARY KEY,  
    RoomPhone VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,  
    AdministratorEmployeeID VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,  
    FOREIGN KEY (AdministratorEmployeeID) REFERENCES Administrators(EmployeeID)  
);  
  
-- 创建管理员表  
CREATE TABLE Administrators (  
    EmployeeID VARCHAR2(20) PRIMARY KEY,  
    Name VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,  
    ContactPhone VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL  
);
```

```sql
-- 插入管理员数据  
INSERT INTO Administrators (EmployeeID, Name, ContactPhone) VALUES ('ADMIN001', 'Admin One', '1234567890');  
INSERT INTO Administrators (EmployeeID, Name, ContactPhone) VALUES ('ADMIN002', 'Admin Two', '0987654321');  
INSERT INTO Administrators (EmployeeID, Name, ContactPhone) VALUES ('ADMIN003', 'Admin Three', '1122334455');  
  
-- 插入管理员数据  
INSERT INTO Administrators (EmployeeID, Name, ContactPhone) VALUES ('ADMIN001', 'Admin One', '1234567890');  
INSERT INTO Administrators (EmployeeID, Name, ContactPhone) VALUES ('ADMIN002', 'Admin Two', '0987654321');  
INSERT INTO Administrators (EmployeeID, Name, ContactPhone) VALUES ('ADMIN003', 'Admin Three', '1122334455');  
  
-- 插入寝室数据  
INSERT INTO Dormitories (DormitoryNumber, RoomPhone, AdministratorEmployeeID) VALUES ('D101', '22233344', 'ADMIN001');  
INSERT INTO Dormitories (DormitoryNumber, RoomPhone, AdministratorEmployeeID) VALUES ('D201', '33344455', 'ADMIN002');  
INSERT INTO Dormitories (DormitoryNumber, RoomPhone, AdministratorEmployeeID) VALUES ('D301', '44455566', 'ADMIN003');  
  
-- 插入学生数据  
INSERT INTO Students (StudentID, Name, Gender, Major, Class, DormitoryNumber, AdministratorEmployeeID) VALUES ('S001', 'Student One', 'M', 'Computer Science', 'CS19', 'D101', 'ADMIN001');  
INSERT INTO Students (StudentID, Name, Gender, Major, Class, DormitoryNumber, AdministratorEmployeeID) VALUES ('S002', 'Student Two', 'F', 'Electrical Engineering', 'EE20', 'D201', 'ADMIN002');  
INSERT INTO Students (StudentID, Name, Gender, Major, Class, DormitoryNumber, AdministratorEmployeeID) VALUES ('S003', 'Student Three', 'M', 'Mathematics', 'MATH18', 'D301', 'ADMIN003');  
INSERT INTO Students (StudentID, Name, Gender, Major, Class, DormitoryNumber, AdministratorEmployeeID) VALUES ('S004', 'Student Four', 'F', 'Physics', 'PHYS19', 'D101', 'ADMIN001');  
  
-- 更新一行学生数据
UPDATE Students SET StudentID = 'S999' WHERE Name = 'Student One';
  
-- 删除一行寝室数据（例如，删除寝室号为'D101'的寝室）  
DELETE FROM Dormitories WHERE DormitoryNumber = 'D101';





-- 查询所有管理员的信息  
SELECT * FROM Administrators;

-- 查询专业为'Computer Science'的学生信息  
SELECT * FROM Students WHERE Major = 'Computer Science';

-- 查询所有管理员及其所管理的寝室信息  
SELECT A.EmployeeID, A.Name AS AdminName, D.DormitoryNumber, D.RoomPhone  
FROM Administrators A  //起别名
JOIN Dormitories D ON A.EmployeeID = D.AdministratorEmployeeID;

-- 查询寝室管理员及其所管理寝室中学生的姓名和专业  
SELECT A.Name AS AdminName, D.DormitoryNumber, S.Name AS StudentName, S.Major  
FROM Administrators A  
JOIN Dormitories D ON A.EmployeeID = D.AdministratorEmployeeID  
JOIN Students S ON D.DormitoryNumber = S.DormitoryNumber;
```

```sql
CREATE TABLE Fleet (  
    FleetID NUMBER PRIMARY KEY,  
    FleetName VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL  
);

CREATE TABLE Vehicle (  
    LicensePlate VARCHAR2(20) PRIMARY KEY,  
    Manufacturer VARCHAR2(100),  
    ManufactureDate DATE,  
    FleetID NUMBER,  
    CONSTRAINT fk_vehicle_fleet FOREIGN KEY (FleetID) REFERENCES Fleet(FleetID)  
);

CREATE TABLE Driver (  
    DriverID NUMBER PRIMARY KEY,  
    Name VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,  
    Phone VARCHAR2(20),  
    ContractPeriod DATE,  
    FleetID NUMBER,  
    CONSTRAINT fk_driver_fleet FOREIGN KEY (FleetID) REFERENCES Fleet(FleetID)  
);

CREATE TABLE Employment (  
    FleetID NUMBER,  
    DriverID NUMBER,  
    ContractPeriod DATE,  
    PRIMARY KEY (FleetID, DriverID, ContractPeriod),  
    CONSTRAINT fk_employment_fleet FOREIGN KEY (FleetID) REFERENCES Fleet(FleetID),  
    CONSTRAINT fk_employment_driver FOREIGN KEY (DriverID) REFERENCES Driver(DriverID)  
);

CREATE TABLE Usage (  
    DriverID NUMBER,  
    LicensePlate VARCHAR2(20),  
    UsageDate DATE,  
    Kilometers NUMBER,  
    PRIMARY KEY (DriverID, LicensePlate, UsageDate),  
    CONSTRAINT fk_usage_driver FOREIGN KEY (DriverID) REFERENCES Driver(DriverID),  
    CONSTRAINT fk_usage_vehicle FOREIGN KEY (LicensePlate) REFERENCES Vehicle(LicensePlate)  
);
```

```sql
-- 车队  
INSERT INTO Fleet (FleetID, FleetName) VALUES (1, 'Fleet A');  
INSERT INTO Fleet (FleetID, FleetName) VALUES (2, 'Fleet B');  

  
-- 车辆  
INSERT INTO Vehicle (LicensePlate, Manufacturer, ManufactureDate, FleetID) VALUES ('ABC123', 'Toyota', TO_DATE('2020-01-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 1);  
  
-- 司机  
INSERT INTO Driver (DriverID, Name, Phone, ContractPeriod, FleetID) VALUES (1, 'John Doe', '1234567890', TO_DATE('2021-01-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 1);  
  
-- 聘用  
INSERT INTO Employment (FleetID, DriverID, ContractPeriod) VALUES (1, 1, TO_DATE('2021-01-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD'));  
  
-- 使用  
INSERT INTO Usage (DriverID, LicensePlate, UsageDate, Kilometers) VALUES (1, 'ABC123', TO_DATE('2021-02-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD'), 100);  


-- 更新一个司机的电话号码  
UPDATE Driver SET Phone = '0987654321' WHERE DriverID = 1;  
  
-- 更新一个车辆的车队  
UPDATE Vehicle SET FleetID = 2 WHERE LicensePlate = 'ABC123';

-- 删除一个聘用记录（请小心使用，这可能会导致引用完整性错误）  
DELETE FROM Employment WHERE FleetID = 1 AND DriverID = 1 AND ContractPeriod = TO_DATE('2021-01-01', 'YYYY-MM-DD');



--查询
SELECT * FROM Fleet;

SELECT * FROM Vehicle WHERE FleetID = 1;
```


# 大作业

## DDL
```sql
-- 创建国家表  
CREATE TABLE COUNTRIES (    
    COUNTRY_ID NUMBER PRIMARY KEY,    
    COUNTRY_NAME VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,    
    REGION VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL    
);    

--创建资源表
CREATE TABLE RESOURCES (  
    COUNTRY_NAME VARCHAR2(100) PRIMARY KEY,       
    YEAR NUMBER,      
    RESOURCE_TYPE VARCHAR2(50),      
    QUANTITY_TYPE VARCHAR2(50),      
    UNIT_TYPE VARCHAR2(50),      
    QUANTITY NUMBER,      
    --FOREIGN KEY (COUNTRY_NAME) REFERENCES COUNTRIES(COUNTRY_NAME),  
);
    
-- 创建石油表  
CREATE TABLE OIL (    
    COUNTRY_NAME VARCHAR2(100),
    YEAR NUMBER,       
    PROVEN_RESERVES_MT NUMBER,  -- 探明储量  
    PRODUCTION_MBBI_PD NUMBER,   -- 日产量（千桶/天，插2020就行
    PRODUCTION_MT_PY NUMBER,   -- 年产量（百万吨）  
    CONSUMPTION_MBBI_PD NUMBER,   -- 日消费量（千桶/天） 
    RP_RATIO NUMBER,        --存储产量比 
    SPOT_PRICE NUMBER        -- 原油现货价格  
    --FOREIGN KEY (COUNTRY_NAME) REFERENCES COUNTRIES(COUNTRY_NAME)  -- 外键关联国家表  
);    

--创建石油产量表
CREATE TABLE OIL_PRODUCTION(
    COUNTRY_NAME VARCHAR2(100),
    YEAR NUMBER,
    PRODUCTION_MT NUMBER, --年产量，百万吨
);

--创建原油现货价格
CREATE TABLE OIL_POTPRICE(
    REGION_SYSTEM VARCHAR2(100),
    YEAR NUMBER,
    SPOT_PRICE_DPB NUMBER, --原油现货价格 ,Dollar per barrel
);

    
-- 创建天然气表  
CREATE TABLE NATURAL_GAS (    
    COUNTRY_NAME VARCHAR2(100),    
    YEAR NUMBER,    
    PRODUCTION_BCM NUMBER,   -- 产量（十亿立方米）  
    CONSUMPTION_BCM NUMBER,  -- 消费量（十亿立方米）     
    --FOREIGN KEY (COUNTRY_NAME) REFERENCES COUNTRIES(COUNTRY_NAME)  -- 外键关联国家表  
);    

    
-- 创建2020年贸易进出口关系表  
CREATE TABLE TRADE_RELATIONS_2020 (    
    EXPORT_COUNTRY VARCHAR2(100),    
    IMPORT_COUNTRY VARCHAR2(100), 
    YEAR NUMBER,
    RESOURCE_TYPE VARCHAR2(50), 
    TRADE_UNIT VARCHAR2(50),
    TRADE_AMOUNT NUMBER
);
--添加限制
ALTER TABLE TRADE_RELATIONS_2020  
ADD CONSTRAINT pk_trade_relations_2020 PRIMARY KEY (EXPORT_COUNTRY, IMPORT_COUNTRY, RESOURCE_TYPE);

--二氧化碳排放表
CREATE TABLE CO2_EMISSION(
    COUNTRY_NAME VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY,
    YEAR NUMBER,
    EMISSION_UNIT VARCHAR(50),
    EMISSION_AMOUNT NUMBER
);

--GDP,人口
CREATE TABLE GDP_POPULATION(
    COUNTRY VARCHAR2(20),
    YEAR NUMBER(10),
    POPULATION NUMBER(10,4),
    GDP NUMBER(10,4)
);

    
-- -- 创建煤炭表  
-- CREATE TABLE COAL (    
--     COUNTRY_ID NUMBER NOT NULL,    
--     YEAR NUMBER NOT NULL,    
--     PROVEN_RESERVES_2020 NUMBER NOT NULL,  -- 2020年底全部探明储量  
--     PRODUCTION NUMBER NOT NULL,            -- 产量  
--     CONSUMPTION NUMBER NOT NULL,           -- 消费量  
--     PRIMARY KEY (COUNTRY_ID, YEAR),    
--     FOREIGN KEY (COUNTRY_ID) REFERENCES COUNTRIES(COUNTRY_ID)  -- 外键关联国家表  
-- );    
    
-- -- 创建碳排放表  
-- CREATE TABLE CARBON (    
--     COUNTRY_ID NUMBER NOT NULL,    
--     YEAR NUMBER NOT NULL,    
--     CO2_EMISSIONS NUMBER NOT NULL,  -- 二氧化碳排放量  
--     PRIMARY KEY (COUNTRY_ID, YEAR),    
--     FOREIGN KEY (COUNTRY_ID) REFERENCES COUNTRIES(COUNTRY_ID)  -- 外键关联国家表  
-- );    
```

# 实验4
```sql
CREATE TABLE GDP_Population(
    COUNTRY VARCHAR(20),
    YEAR NUMBER(10),
    Population NUMBER(10,4),
    GDP NUMBER(10,4)
);
```
## 1
```sql
SELECT     
    COUNTRY,    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2010 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2010",    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2011 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2011",    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2012 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2012",    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2013 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2013",    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2014 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2014",    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2015 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2015",    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2016 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2016",    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2017 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2017",    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2018 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2018",    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2019 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2019",    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2020 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2020",    
    SUM(GDP) AS 总计    
FROM     
    GDP_Population    
WHERE     
    COUNTRY IN ('中国', '美国', '英国', '法国', '俄罗斯联邦', '印度', '日本', '瑞典', '德国')    
    AND YEAR BETWEEN 2010 AND 2020    
GROUP BY     
    COUNTRY    
ORDER BY     
    COUNTRY;
```


## 2
```sql
SELECT     
    COUNTRY,    
    SUM(DECODE(YEAR, 2010, GDP, 0)) AS "2010",    
    SUM(DECODE(YEAR, 2011, GDP, 0)) AS "2011",    
    SUM(DECODE(YEAR, 2012, GDP, 0)) AS "2012",    
    SUM(DECODE(YEAR, 2013, GDP, 0)) AS "2013",    
    SUM(DECODE(YEAR, 2014, GDP, 0)) AS "2014",    
    SUM(DECODE(YEAR, 2015, GDP, 0)) AS "2015",    
    SUM(DECODE(YEAR, 2016, GDP, 0)) AS "2016",    
    SUM(DECODE(YEAR, 2017, GDP, 0)) AS "2017",    
    SUM(DECODE(YEAR, 2018, GDP, 0)) AS "2018",    
    SUM(DECODE(YEAR, 2019, GDP, 0)) AS "2019",    
    SUM(DECODE(YEAR, 2020, GDP, 0)) AS "2020",    
    SUM(GDP) AS 总计    
FROM     
    GDP_Population    
WHERE     
    COUNTRY IN ('中国', '美国', '英国', '法国', '俄罗斯联邦', '印度', '日本', '瑞典', '德国')    
    AND YEAR BETWEEN 2010 AND 2020    
GROUP BY     
    COUNTRY    
ORDER BY     
    COUNTRY;
```



## 3
```sql
SELECT v1.*, v2.总计 
FROM (    
    SELECT COUNTRY, YEAR, GDP    
    FROM GDP_Population    

    WHERE COUNTRY IN ('中国', '美国', '英国', '法国', '俄罗斯联邦', '印度', '日本', '瑞典', '德国')    
      AND YEAR BETWEEN 2010 AND 2020    
)    
PIVOT (     
    SUM(GDP)    
    FOR YEAR IN (     
        2010 AS "2010",   
        2011 AS "2011",   
        2012 AS "2012",   
        2013 AS "2013",   
        2014 AS "2014",     
        2015 AS "2015",   
        2016 AS "2016",   
        2017 AS "2017",   
        2018 AS "2018",   
        2019 AS "2019",     
        2020 AS "2020"  
    )    
) v1
JOIN (
    SELECT
        COUNTRY,
        SUM(GDP) AS 总计  
    FROM GDP_Population 
    GROUP BY COUNTRY
) v2 ON v1.COUNTRY = v2.COUNTRY
ORDER BY v1.COUNTRY;

    

```

## 4
```sql
SELECT     
    COUNTRY,       
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2016 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2016",    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2017 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2017",    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2018 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2018",    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2019 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2019",    
    SUM(CASE WHEN YEAR = 2020 THEN GDP ELSE 0 END) AS "2020",    
    SUM(GDP) AS 总计    
FROM     
    GDP_Population    
WHERE     
    COUNTRY IN ('中国', '美国', '英国', '法国', '俄罗斯联邦', '印度', '日本', '瑞典', '德国')    
    AND YEAR BETWEEN 2016 AND 2020    
GROUP BY     
    COUNTRY    
ORDER BY     
    COUNTRY;
```

## 5
```sql
SELECT *    
FROM (    
    SELECT COUNTRY, YEAR, GDP    
    FROM GDP_Population    

    WHERE COUNTRY IN ('中国', '美国', '英国', '法国', '俄罗斯联邦', '印度', '日本', '瑞典', '德国')    
      AND YEAR BETWEEN 2016 AND 2020    
)    
PIVOT (     
    SUM(GDP)    
    FOR YEAR IN (        
        2016 AS "2016",   
        2017 AS "2017",   
        2018 AS "2018",   
        2019 AS "2019",     
        2020 AS "2020"  
    )    
)    
ORDER BY COUNTRY;
```

## 6
```sql
SELECT v1.*, v2.总计 
FROM (    
    SELECT COUNTRY, YEAR, GDP    
    FROM GDP_Population    

    WHERE COUNTRY IN ('中国', '美国', '英国', '法国', '俄罗斯联邦', '印度', '日本', '瑞典', '德国')    
      AND YEAR BETWEEN 2016 AND 2020    
)    
PIVOT (     
    SUM(GDP)    
    FOR YEAR IN (       
        2016 AS "2016",   
        2017 AS "2017",   
        2018 AS "2018",   
        2019 AS "2019",     
        2020 AS "2020"  
    )    
) v1
JOIN (
    SELECT
        COUNTRY,
        SUM(GDP) AS 总计  
    FROM GDP_Population 
    WHERE YEAR BETWEEN 2016 AND 2020
    GROUP BY COUNTRY
) v2 ON v1.COUNTRY = v2.COUNTRY
ORDER BY v1.COUNTRY;
```
    
## 7 
```sql
WITH PerCapitaGDP AS (  
    SELECT   
        COUNTRY,  
        YEAR,  
        GDP / Population AS PerCapitaGDP 
    FROM   
        GDP_Population  
    WHERE   
        COUNTRY IN ('中国', '美国', '英国', '法国', '俄罗斯联邦', '印度', '日本', '瑞典', '德国')  
        AND YEAR BETWEEN 2010 AND 2020  
        AND Population <> 0 
)  
SELECT *  
FROM PerCapitaGDP  
PIVOT (  
    AVG(PerCapitaGDP)  
    FOR YEAR IN (2010 AS "2010", 2011 AS "2011", 2012 AS "2012", 2013 AS "2013", 2014 AS "2014",   
                 2015 AS "2015", 2016 AS "2016", 2017 AS "2017", 2018 AS "2018", 2019 AS "2019",   
                 2020 AS "2020")  
)  
ORDER BY COUNTRY;
```

## 8
```sql
WITH PerCapitaGDP AS (  
    SELECT   
        COUNTRY,  
        YEAR,  
        ROUND(GDP / Population * 1000,2) AS PerCapitaGDP 
    FROM   
        GDP_Population  
    WHERE   
        COUNTRY IN ('中国', '美国', '英国', '法国', '俄罗斯联邦', '印度', '日本', '瑞典', '德国')  
        AND YEAR BETWEEN 2010 AND 2020  
        AND Population <> 0 
)  
SELECT *  
FROM PerCapitaGDP  
PIVOT (  
    AVG(PerCapitaGDP)  
    FOR YEAR IN (2010 AS "2010", 2011 AS "2011", 2012 AS "2012", 2013 AS "2013", 2014 AS "2014",   
                 2015 AS "2015", 2016 AS "2016", 2017 AS "2017", 2018 AS "2018", 2019 AS "2019",   
                 2020 AS "2020")  
)  
ORDER BY COUNTRY;
```

# 期末作业
## DDL
```sql
CREATE TABLE RE_人口 (
    year NUMBER PRIMARY KEY, 
    total_population NUMBER, 
    male_population NUMBER, 
    female_population NUMBER, 
    urban_population NUMBER, 
    rural_population NUMBER, 
    average_annual_wage NUMBER
);

CREATE TABLE RE_estate_employment (
    year NUMBER PRIMARY KEY,                      -- 时间（年）
    average_employment NUMBER,                     -- 房地产开发企业平均从业人数（人）
    average_employment_domestic NUMBER,            -- 内资房地产开发企业平均从业人数（人）
    average_employment_state_owned NUMBER,          -- 国有房地产开发企业平均从业人数（人）
    average_employment_collective NUMBER,          -- 集体房地产开发企业平均从业人数（人）
    average_employment_hmt NUMBER,                 -- 港、澳、台投资房地产开发企业平均从业人数（人）
    average_employment_foreign NUMBER,             -- 外商投资房地产开发企业平均从业人数（人）
    enterprise_count NUMBER,                       -- 房地产开发企业个数（个）
    enterprise_count_domestic NUMBER,               -- 内资房地产开发企业个数（个）
    enterprise_count_state_owned NUMBER,            -- 国有房地产开发企业个数（个）
    enterprise_count_collective NUMBER,            -- 集体房地产开发企业个数（个）
    enterprise_count_hmt NUMBER,                    -- 港、澳、台投资房地产开发企业个数（个）
    enterprise_count_foreign NUMBER                -- 外商投资房地产开发企业个数（个）
);

CREATE TABLE RE_estate_investment (
    year NUMBER PRIMARY KEY,                      -- 时间（年）
    total_fixed_asset_investment NUMBER,           --全社会固定资产投资（亿元）
    fixed_asset_investment_exc_rural NUMBER,      --固定资产投资(不含农户)（亿元）
    real_estate_investment NUMBER,                --房地产开发投资（亿元）
    new_start_area_residential NUMBER,            --房地产开发企业新开工房屋面积（万平方米）
    new_start_area_residential_only NUMBER,       --房地产开发企业住宅新开工房屋面积（万平方米）
    new_start_area_villas_premium_apartments NUMBER,--房地产开发企业别墅、高档公寓新开工房屋面积（万平方米）
    new_start_area_offices NUMBER,                --房地产开发企业办公楼新开工房屋面积（万平方米）
    new_start_area_commercial NUMBER,              --房地产开发企业商业营业用房新开工房屋面积（万平方米）
    new_start_area_others NUMBER,                 --房地产开发企业其他用途新开工房屋面积（万平方米）
    average_sales_price_commercial NUMBER,         --商品房平均销售价格（元/平方米）
    average_sales_price_residential NUMBER,       --住宅商品房平均销售价格（元/平方米）
    average_sales_price_villas_premium_apartments NUMBER, --别墅、高档公寓平均销售价格（元/平方米）
    average_sales_price_offices NUMBER,           --办公楼商品房平均销售价格（元/平方米）
    average_sales_price_commercial_only NUMBER,    --商业营业用房平均销售价格（元/平方米）
    average_sales_price_others NUMBER             --其他商品房平均销售价格（元/平方米）
);

CREATE TABLE total_fixed_investment (
    year NUMBER PRIMARY KEY,                      -- 时间（年）
    total_investment NUMBER(15, 2),                -- 全社会固定资产投资（亿元）
    investment_exc_rural NUMBER(15, 2),           -- 固定资产投资(不含农户)（亿元）
    real_estate_investment NUMBER(15, 2),         -- 房地产开发投资（亿元）
    private_investment NUMBER(15, 2),              -- 民间固定资产（不含农户）投资额（亿元）
    private_investment_ratio NUMBER(5, 2)          -- 民间固定资产（不含农户）投资额占固定资产投资(不含农户)比重（%）
);

CREATE TABLE engel_coefficient (
    year NUMBER PRIMARY KEY,                      -- 时间（年）
    resident_engel_coefficient NUMBER(3,1),        -- 居民恩格尔系数（%）
    urban_resident_engel_coefficient NUMBER(3,1),   -- 城镇居民恩格尔系数（%）
    rural_resident_engel_coefficient NUMBER(3,1)    -- 农村居民恩格尔系数（%）
);
```

## 查询

1. 简单查询：获取2023年的总人口和城镇人口。
SELECT total_population, urban_population
FROM RE_人口
WHERE year = 2023;

2. 分组查询：计算每个年份段的平均房地产开发投资额。
SELECT year,
   AVG(real_estate_investment) AS avg_investment
FROM RE_estate_investment
GROUP BY year;
3. 分组查询（含Having子句）：找出平均恩格尔系数低于30%的年份。
SELECT year, AVG(resident_engel_coefficient) AS avg_engel_coefficient
FROM engel_coefficient
GROUP BY year
HAVING AVG(resident_engel_coefficient) < 30;
4. 相关子查询：获取投资额超过平均投资额的所有年份和投资额。
SELECT year, total_investment
FROM total_fixed_investment
WHERE total_investment > (SELECT AVG(total_investment) FROM total_fixed_investment);
5. 连接查询：获取每个年份的城镇人口和恩格尔系数，并按年份排序。
SELECT e.year, p.urban_population, e.urban_resident_engel_coefficient
FROM engel_coefficient e
JOIN RE_人口 p ON e.year = p.year
ORDER BY e.year;
6. 外连接查询：获取所有年份的房地产投资数据，包括没有对应房地产投资记录的年份。
SELECT i.year, i.real_estate_investment, e.enterprise_count
FROM RE_estate_investment i
LEFT JOIN RE_estate_employment e ON i.year = e.year
ORDER BY i.year;
7. 转置查询：将不同类型房地产新开工房屋面积按年份转置显示。
SELECT
  year,
  MAX(CASE WHEN type = 'residential' THEN new_start_area ELSE 0 END) AS residential_area,
  MAX(CASE WHEN type = 'villas_premium_apartments' THEN new_start_area ELSE 0 END) AS villas_area,
  MAX(CASE WHEN type = 'offices' THEN new_start_area ELSE 0 END) AS offices_area,
  MAX(CASE WHEN type = 'commercial' THEN new_start_area ELSE 0 END) AS commercial_area,
  MAX(CASE WHEN type = 'others' THEN new_start_area ELSE 0 END) AS others_area
FROM (
  SELECT
    year,
    new_start_area_residential AS new_start_area,
    'residential' AS type
  FROM RE_estate_investment
  UNION ALL
  SELECT
    year,
    new_start_area_villas_premium_apartments,
    'villas_premium_apartments' AS type
  FROM RE_estate_investment
  UNION ALL
  SELECT
    year,
    new_start_area_offices,
    'offices' AS type
  FROM RE_estate_investment
  UNION ALL
  SELECT
    year,
    new_start_area_commercial,
    'commercial' AS type
  FROM RE_estate_investment
  UNION ALL
  SELECT
    year,
    new_start_area_others,
    'others' AS type
  FROM RE_estate_investment
) subquery
GROUP BY year
ORDER BY year;
8. 分组查询：计算每个年份段的固定资产投资总额，并按总额降序排列。
SELECT year,
  SUM(total_investment) AS total_investment_sum
FROM total_fixed_investment
GROUP BY year
ORDER BY total_investment_sum DESC;
9. 相关子查询：找出民间固定资产投资额占固定资产投资(不含农户)比重最高的年份。
SELECT year, private_investment_ratio
FROM total_fixed_investment
WHERE private_investment_ratio = (SELECT MAX(private_investment_ratio) FROM total_fixed_investment);
10. 分组查询：获取每个年份的平均房地产开发企业平均从业人数，并按平均从业人数降序排列。
SELECT year, AVG(average_employment) AS avg_employment
FROM RE_estate_employment
GROUP BY year
ORDER BY avg_employment DESC;
11.简单查询：计算平均年工资与平均房价的比值
SELECT
  人口.year AS year, -- 假设 'year' 字段在 'RE_人口' 表中
  人口.average_annual_wage AS average_annual_wage, -- 假设 'average_annual_wage' 在 'RE_人口' 表中
  投资.average_sales_price_commercial AS average_house_price -- 假设 'average_sales_price_commercial' 在 'RE_estate_investment' 表中
FROM
  RE_人口 人口
JOIN
  RE_estate_investment 投资
ON
  人口.year = 投资.year;

12.转置查询：获取不同类型房地产平均销售价格按年份转置显示。
SELECT
  year,
  MAX(CASE WHEN type = 'average_employment_domestic' THEN average_employment ELSE 0 END) AS "内资企业平均从业人数",
  MAX(CASE WHEN type = 'average_employment_state_owned' THEN average_employment ELSE 0 END) AS "国有企业平均从业人数",
  MAX(CASE WHEN type = 'average_employment_collective' THEN average_employment ELSE 0 END) AS "集体企业平均从业人数",
  MAX(CASE WHEN type = 'average_employment_hmt' THEN average_employment ELSE 0 END) AS "港、澳、台投资企业平均从业人数",
  MAX(CASE WHEN type = 'average_employment_foreign' THEN average_employment ELSE 0 END) AS "外商投资企业平均从业人数"
FROM (
  SELECT
    year,
    average_employment_domestic AS average_employment,
    'average_employment_domestic' AS type
  FROM RE_estate_employment
  UNION ALL
  SELECT
    year,
    average_employment_state_owned,
    'average_employment_state_owned' AS type
  FROM RE_estate_employment
  UNION ALL
  SELECT
    year,
    average_employment_collective,
    'average_employment_collective' AS type
  FROM RE_estate_employment
  UNION ALL
  SELECT
    year,
    average_employment_hmt,
    'average_employment_hmt' AS type
  FROM RE_estate_employment
  UNION ALL
  SELECT
    year,
    average_employment_foreign,
    'average_employment_foreign' AS type
  FROM RE_estate_employment
) employment_types
GROUP BY year
ORDER BY year;

# pl/sql
DECLARE
    v_population_growth NUMBER;
    v_wage_growth NUMBER;
    v_start_year NUMBER := 2014; -- 假设2014年为起始年份
    v_end_year NUMBER := 2022; -- 假设2023年为结束年份
    v_start_population NUMBER;
    v_start_wage NUMBER;
    v_end_population NUMBER;
    v_end_wage NUMBER;
BEGIN
    -- 获取起始年份的人口和工资
    SELECT total_population, average_annual_wage INTO v_start_population, v_start_wage
    FROM RE_人口
    WHERE year = v_start_year;
    
    -- 获取结束年份的人口和工资
    SELECT total_population, average_annual_wage INTO v_end_population, v_end_wage
    FROM RE_人口
    WHERE year = v_end_year;
    
    -- 计算人口和工资的增长
    v_population_growth := (v_end_population - v_start_population) / v_start_population * 100;
    v_wage_growth := (v_end_wage - v_start_wage) / v_start_wage * 100;
    
    -- 输出统计解读
    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('从' || v_start_year || '年到' || v_end_year || '年，人口增长了' || 
                         ROUND(v_population_growth, 2) || '%，平均年工资增长了' || 
                         ROUND(v_wage_growth, 2) || '%。');
END;
/
